< text>
Took way too long for a pair of "in stock" skates to be shipped. Customer service communications definitely did not make me feel like a valued customer. I regret apologizing for feeling like I was bothering them and somehow being annoyed for their terrible email response time. Then it took them forever to ship my order. I will not be shopping from them again in the future.

Furthermore, I ordered the Moxie Panthers, and the leopard toe caps didn't come with them. They did put in a crab tool, but it didn't fit any of my skate wheel or truck nuts, so I ordered another crab tool along with my Luminous wheels, from Eastern Skating Supply.

If you want fast shipping and more in stock choices go to Eastern Skating Supply online or RollerSkateNation.com. Both have excellent service and faster shipping.</text>

< Review>
Great skates, but don't order them online directly from their website - go through amazon or something. I never post reviews about anything ever but I felt this needed to be said. This whole experience left a bad taste in my mouth and makes me not even want to skate anymore.

I pre-ordered the green (honeydew) color on June 12th and assumed they would ship when the skates officially released (June 14th I think), because that's how pre-orders are supposed to work. I also ordered a set of trick wheels on or around June 16th.

The confirmation e-mail they send when you place an order says "it takes 2-3 business days to process your order once it has been placed and 2 days to ship," unless they're out of stock, then they'll notify you. The e-mail also says the skates can take 1-5 weeks to make if they're not it stock. I assumed I wouldn't have to deal with any of that because, again, I placed a pre-order.

On June 26th, 2 WEEKS after not hearing anything, I e-mailed them and asked if there were any updates. After e-mailing several times, I didn't get a response until July 2nd (a week later), and was told that if I ordered after April 1st the skates would ship out in the order they were purchased... That's doesn't sound like a pre-order to me.

On July 18th I was done waiting and proceeded to cancel my orders (both the trick wheels and the skates). I would order a different color through amazon instead. The trick wheel order was canceled the same day, the skates were not.

I e-mailed again on July 20th asking them to cancel my skate order. July 25th, I WAS TOLD MY SKATES HAD ALREADY SHIPPED AND THEY COULDN'T CANCEL THE ORDER. What!? That really pissed me off - you can cancel the wheels the same day but you wait until it's too late to cancel the skates? I honestly feel like they stole my money.

I finally received my skates on July 27th.

TL;DR - IT TOOK ME OVER 6 WEEKS TO GET MY SKATES, EVEN THOUGH I PRE-ORDERED THEM. Their customer service is sporadic at best - sometimes I would get an e-mail back the same day and other times weeks later - which ended up costing me hundreds of dollars for an extra pair of skates that I now have to send back to amazon (which I received in less than a week btw, shout out to amazon).

Thank you for reading, I hope this review helps someone.

edit: I'm sorry, but for the sake of visibility, I cannot remove this review. The online shop and physical store are connected as far as branding goes - it's all the same from a customer's perspective. I did also leave this review on yelp and have seen other reviews cross-posted in both places as well (about the online shop and the location).

Either way, I was not confused, I was mislead. On the website, the summer color listings had "pre-order" in the title until June 14th, which would lead anyone to believe they would get their skates just like any other pre-order up until that date. Moxi should've been much clearer about what a pre-order means for a small business with handmade items, as it is not common knowledge. They could've done that in a number of ways (ex. through social media, in the description of the listing, etc.), so there is no excuse. Thank you.< /Review>

<date>1564422376208<//date>< Text>
This pho place was a lot nicer and cleaner than most I've been to. The restaurant was decently sized and there was even a bar. I used a yelp deal and got Cajun garlic truffle fries with my pho tai (rare steak). There were so many different flavored fries! I love that these fries were thin and crispy. The ones I got were kind of spicy but there were other flavors you could have gotten too! I chose the Cajun garlic truffle because they were literally all the flavors I love on my fries and I've NEVER seen fries with all three seasonings!! I would come back just for the fries. You could just order the fries for $3 also.

I was hungry so I got the pho. The meat was pretty tough but I'm not sure if it was just my pho or if it's normally like that. I honestly think the fries are better than the pho... but I have a bias towards fries as you can tell. Overall, I would come here again to eat</Text>

< review>
Like many of us in the Bay Area, we‚Äôre in one of the post war building boom homes built in the late 50‚Äôs. The roof design of many of these these homes have the rafters extending so far out the edge that they block quite a bit of sunlight coming through the windows, leaving the homes dark and dreary inside. These solar tubes are wonderful in that they require minimal cuts in your roof and ceiling, compared to traditional skylights, preserving the integrity of your roof. The light they produce is on par with a traditional skylight. The added benefit of solar night lights, plus the ability to add a light fixture for lighting the area at night, makes this an all around solution for lighting those dark areas in these older homes.

The installation team was very nice, professional, and was in and out in 90 minutes. I look forward to their installing more of these light in my home.< /review>

I had two solar tubes installed. One in the living room and the other in the hall way.
The one in the living room was positioned toward the back of the wall, and away
from the front window.  The results were spectacular.  As the sun's light diminished in the afternoon, the back part of living room would become dismally dimmed. I also had a solar exhaust fan installed in the attic to help fan out the build up of hot air during the hot days of summer. < text>
The Sunlight Concepts' installers arrived at our home 1/2-hour earlier than scheduled!   They were very knowledgeable about the products and answered all of my questions.

The original plan was to have 2-"1600" solar powered attic fans installed on our roof.  When one of the installers suggested that I have an additional "1200" solar powered attic fan installed on our garage roof, I happily agreed as the garage faces the afternoon sun and gets very warm inside, during the summer months!  I also opted to have  thermostat controls wired into the fans' circuits, so the fans will not operate when the ambient temperature in the attic is less than 85 degrees.  (The thermostats will prolong the life of the fan motors.)  Even with the installation of the additional fan and the thermostat controls, the installers completed the install in less than 45 minutes.  They cleaned up all of the debris and took away all of the packaging materials.  The installers were very polite and did an excellent job in the installations.

From the front of the house, I can only see a small portion of a fan housing peeking over the ridge of the roof.  The other 2-fans are hidden from street-view.  We didn't have very  many hot days this past summer, but during the few warm days, our house remained comfortably cool.  The garage and laundry room were noticeably cooler than in past years!  The 2-attic fans over the living space of our home can not be heard while operating.  Even the fan on the garage roof is very quiet and I can see the bottom of the fan housing and the spinning blades, from inside the garage.</text>

I trained with Anthony N. for 6 months and had the best experience at Perform For Life. Prior to starting, I had been recovering from a series of injuries to both my lower and upper half of my body, so I was a out of shape and had only finished my Physical Therapy a few months prior. I highly recommend Perform For Life (regardless of the location) if you are somehow who is looking for an intimate training session with a knowledgeable fitness specialist, or looking for a small group training class that is not 30+ people piled into a room.

<UserId.>106819911432904458614</UserId.><Name>Sam Geffner</Name>< Time>
1493676377582<//Time>
< rating>
5</rating>
<Text>Recently I told Amber how pleased I was with our work together.  Through my work with her over the months, I have begun to make the transition from a person who had to go to exercise to help improve the odds of keeping my cancer in check, to a person who is beginning to think of exercise as a part of my personality and a valued lifestyle choice.
Amber shows unusual skill in gauging the exercises to my ability.  It often seems as if she starts a set of exercises with a low-ball warm-up resistance.  In subsequent sets I get to request more weight.  That experience of wanting to do more, to work harder is, for me, a unique experience around exercise.   By low-balling resistance and working up, Amber models and teaches a kind of patience that I had never associated with exercise and allows me to experience a quite novel experience in myself of eagerness around exercise combined with patience about the results.  Despite my impatience with her cautious approach, I often wind up feeling manageable muscle soreness after workouts which makes me feel just a bit of the self-righteous and heroic warrior.

Amber shows unexpected inventiveness in hitting the same basic muscle groups in novel ways as well as a consistency of attention to proper form which is unaccustomed to me.  This keeps my workouts interesting and also works all possible associated peripheral muscles. It also contributes to the impression that she really thinks hard about how to make the workouts interesting and entertaining.  She is also so consistent about monitoring the basics of good body mechanics that I now anticipate the corrections she is about to make.  This makes it easier to integrate our training into my daily activity.  For example, I now experience brisk walking as an exercise in awareness in balancing the demands on my legs and calves with my buttocks and back chain.  When lifting, I remind myself to anchor my lats and pay attention to not over-stressing my shoulder joints.  Over the months, my posture has greatly improved, and friends tell me that I am looking much stronger.

Amber is unexpectedly organized in the way that she presents her exercises. She typically starts with warm-ups, presents the main core of our workouts in in sets of 2 or 3 exercises targeting opposing muscle groups, each set repeated three times before moving on to the next set.  She finishes with some playful cool-downs and balance exercises.  This gives me a way to think about the structure of a workout session which has been very helpful to me in beginning to explore working out at home.

Amber's personality and attitudes present a good fit with my personality needs, which has been very helpful in encouraging me to think of exercise as an enjoyable part of my lifestyle.  She is professional about maintaining some distance between her needs and mine, yet not so distant that I don't feel that I have come to know her as a person and feel a sense of her genuine caring and playfulness.  She has skillfully managed all the negative personality traits and unproductive attitudes that I brought to exercise.  For example, each workout she cheerfully and genuinely encourages me to complain about whatever is interfering with my desire to exercise - and then tells me to get going.  She models using one's body with all its limitations as best as one can at the time.  Again and again, I have had the experience of coming in grumpy and unmotivated and leaving feeling energized and successful.  An experienced exerciser may take this for granted, but believe me, this experience is unaccustomed in my life, especially as I have aged and since my cancer treatment.

To the extent possible, I think that Amber brings a quality of broad knowledge, professional attitudes, consistent effort, and playfulness  to our workouts that encourages me to think about my daily activities as potential opportunities to reinforce my workouts and to gladly integrate exercise more deeply into my life.  And that is what Perform for Life is all about.<//Text>< Pics>
